should use a secondary wikipedia tag - linking to a violation of law
linked wikidata entry (Q369336) is about a violation of law, so it is very unlikely to be correct
subject:wikipedia=* or subject:wikipedia tag would be probably better (see https://wiki.openstreetmap.org/wiki/Key:wikipedia#Secondary_Wikipedia_links for full list of what else may be applicable)
in case of change remember to remove wikidata tag if it is present
